s.sectors||[];\n  if(_treeDim==='co')return s.countries||[];\n  if(_treeDim==='grp')return s.groups||[];\n  if(_treeDim==='rank')return(s.ranks||[]).map(r=>({n:r.l||'Q'+r.r,p:r.p,b:0,a:r.a}));\n if(_treeDim==='grp')return h.subg;\n  if(_treeDim==='rank'){\n    // Quintile based on overall rank score\n    let r=h.over;if(r==null)return null;\n    return['Q1 (Best)','Q2','Q3','Q4','Q5 (Worst)'][Math.min(Math.max(Math.round(r)-1,0),4)];\n  }\n  return null;\n}\n\n// Continuous color scale: intense green for strong OW, intense red for strong UW, muted near zero\nfunction _treeColor(activeWt){\n  let a=activeWt||0;\n  let intensity=Math.min(Math.abs(a)/5,1); // full intensity at +/-5%\n  if(a>=0){\n    let r=Math.round(16+(1-intensity)*14);\n    let g=Math.round(185-(1-intensity)*50);\n    let b=Math.round(129-(1-intensity)*40);\n    return`rgb(${r},${g},${b})`;\n  } else {\n    let r=Math.round(239-(1-intensity)*50);\n    let _treeHeatColor(teContr,maxTE){\n  if(!maxTE||maxTE===0)return'#334155';\n  let intensity=Math.min(Math.abs(teContr)/maxTE,1);\n  let r=Math.round(30+intensity*69);  // 30 → 99\n  let
